108453675463629554167< /user_id>
< Review>
One of 6 Starbucks in Danville. This one is right across the street from San Ramon Valley High. Be prepared to be with surrounded by teens after school during the year.

Staff is friendly and attentive. Happy to take and deliver custom coffee offers with a smile.

Place could be a little cleaner, but this is a high foot traffic location from the school and being in Danville Square (across the parking lot from TJs) with the surround neighborhood it also serves. Hence, one less star.

Sells and serves all the usual things found at a Starbucks -- coffee and frappuccinos, teas pastries, prepared foods - sandwiches, canned drinks, Starbucks merchandise and coffee beans, etc.

Plenty of seating (tables, comfy leather chairs) indoors and outdoors with big umbrellas to help block out the Danville sun. Free wifi. Has an area to pick up mobile phone orders.

Pleasantly surprised to see 2 unisex / ADA restrooms. So there is never a line for a particular gender. Only con - no diaper changing table in either unisex restroom. = (

Parking, including handicapped parking can be found within the Danville Square parking lot. It also be tough to find a parking space throughout the week depending during the hour of day.

8/30/2019 Update: During the school year, it can get crowded and very loud once SRVHS lets out - the students walk over and start ordering!</Review>

< Review>
This Starbucks Reserve location is a relatively new family oriented location which I frequent almost every day. Filled with kids, dogs and friends it is a happy place to be!

That being said - I wish they would maintain the outside patio which is often strewn with garbage from the overflowing recycling containers. There are leaves everywhere, underneath all the tables and chairs which are infrequently cleaned up. Not a chore for any employee.

Seems to me that this patio which has the ability to seat 40 to 50 should be pristine as it borders the the sidewalk and main drag in Danville - Hartz Ave. Hopefully management will see this post, can only improve what is already a very good Starbucks!< /Review>

<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
Not sure what the last was talking about? Humanist Hall is really interesting! Read the history for god sakes! This Hall is one of the last cool spaces for rent in rapidly gentrifying Oakland which doesn't cost thousands of dollars! It has a wonderful main room with art deco light fixtures and vaulted beam ceilings, a full kitchen, two bathrooms (one is ADA), walkable to BART, and lots of street parking for Oakland. Geesh, what more can you ask for? Oh, I forgot to mention the amazing, large back yard! Evil property developers want to tear down this historic hall to put in more crappy condos. I hope that never happens cause Humanist Hall is a public service to the people of Oakland!</Text>

<user_id>108685370139018629938< /user_id><Name>Jay Keyes<//Name><Date>1577644717835</Date>< Rate>
5<//Rate>
<text>The specialty of Tito's La Especial are "tacos al vapor," aka steamed tacos. This delicious Mexican street food is also known as "tacos de canasta" (basket tacos) because they're traditionally layered in a big basket and sold by street vendors, many of whom hawk them from their bikes.

Tito's "Carne Deshebrada Taco Al Vapor" is excellent. Aside from steamed double corn tortillas comprising each taco's "shell," the chile-steeped shredded beef inside is soft, luscious, and as juicy as you'd want any meat to be. You do want to eat these quickly, before the tortillas begin to stick to the wrappers they are served in. Despite the fact they traditionally would be drizzled in oil (to help preserve them) and served out of a basket over the course of a day, these tacos are best made-to-order. I would also recommend the "Papas Taco Al Vapor," consisting of seasoned potatoes in a ranchera sauce, a loose mash of creamy crushed potatoes and firmer chunks, all colored orange from the sauce.

The "Taco Dorado de Carne Deshebrada" served here is the complete opposite of the al vapor tacos, as the tortilla is instead a crunchy deep-fried shell that is stuffed with stewed beef, lettuce, chopped tomatoes, and shredded cheese. Tito's does a decent job with this style of taco, but you really should stick to the al vapor tacos here, which are indeed "especial."

Tito's La Especial's salsa roja is made of fire and miracles and I recommend it be used on everything you eat here.< /text><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOi1XyvPqLMkx0USiLiN0vgmzc5PMbnZW3Zy3ED=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM_dAf952Lp4CXpcj4EwFcNvHGr-eCJOp448So4=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOAYocEnhdaptirVQEh4DqxQSODPVCsZxAcPPTM=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOmw0hZELb3PP9-z00K5BA2keJCNZX3kVLjolEJ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMw9TlAN-w6GJWCQ6JIhyyPOrIAANMX0txnpuUC=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOuAPcu6Jxdai3CiIrWyAHKoYOkR58VdEZOULRA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNWXyYMOG3ZTjrLRaZPdPz2oMdCtwMyEkqf9Mw6=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics><Resp>None< /Resp>< Gmap_id>
